<Author>Teutonic
<Content>Perfect We stayed here on route to NZ for 2 nights and it was absolutely perfect. From the initial walking in to cool air and fountains, to the enormous reception area and friendly staff. The room was totally immaculate, tastefully decorated with an amazing view. The bathroom was fantastic - large, with a waterfall shower that we didn't want to get out of. The hotel had a very well equipped gym, with running machines, free weights etc and 2 beautiful pools which we spent a good few hours by. The hotel sits on top of a very impressive shopping centre with numerous restaurants, while a huge food court is just over the road. It is almost next door to all the fun of the old Raffles so you can waste money buying overpriced, but very nice Singapore Slings and throw peanut shells all over the floor. If there was a downside it was the walk into the city district but cabs are so cheap that really is not an issue. I actually cannot fault this hotel at all, very rare for me and have given it 5 stars, even though I think other Tripadvisor members are too quick to give the maximum. I will stay here every time I go to Singapore, without fail.

<Author>Benjybobber
<Content>Excellent Hotel We stayed at Raffles the Plaza for 6 nights and had an excellent time. The staff were extremely friendly, particularly towards the children. The pool area was great, with two good sized pools and plenty of sunbeds, although sunbathing was a little difficult due to the height of the two hotel towers overlooking the pool. We were upgraded to the Raffles Inc floor and had access to the lounge for guests on that floor - though I couldn't really see the point of it as it was always empty and the breakfast served in the restaurant had a much better choice. The Hotel is well located to access the city. There is a MRT station in a shopping complex attached to the Hotel. Taxis are extremely cheap and probably more convenient. We would definitely stay at Raffles the Plaza again.

<Author>Dreaming_of_Elysium
<Content>Fab stay at the Raffles Plaza, fantastic value for money! We arrrived at the Raffles Plaza at a very busy time of day around 6.30pm and the checkin staff were all busy and little queues had started to form to check in at the main desk. My friend and I were very tired after an early flight from Sydney and were very relieved when Berm on the adjacent customer service desk beckoned us to check in at his desk. He took great care to check and fulfiil our requirements and searched untill he found a very nice room to which he gave us a complimentary upgrade, and extended our check- out time to 3pm without charge as we had a midnight flight back to the UK. We had a lovely deluxe room in the South Tower which had the most fantastic view of the esplanade, harbour and sea, just the view that every weary newly arrived visitor yearns to find when opening the curtains (which incidently opened by remote control from a little panel by each bed). The window was truly enormous floor to ceiling and wall to wall with a balcony. The rooms are ultra modern as is the foyer and the bathrooms have to be seen to be believed with glass basins and shelving, and the most lovely rainfall shower that drenches you and is really refreshing  Raffles own toiletries that were relaced reqularly. A nice touch was the daily compliementary bottles of water in the room and iced water at the pool bar. The pool area was lovely with two big circular pools (shared with the Stamford next door, which incidentaly had all the charm of an airport departure lounge due to the constant coming and goings of air crew who stay there) and at least some of the sunbeds had the sun all day(grab the ones at the Stamford end, by beating the British Air crew to them.) The breakfast was great in the Market Cafet, better in my opinion than the Intercontinental where we stayed on the outward leg of our trip to Austrailia, we didnt fancy the Aligator Pear pool breakfast area as it is outdoor and with the heat and humidity is not ideal. Nice touch to have sound system in the room, try the preset chanel 5 for nice chilled out music to relax to. In my opinion the location is second to none, it is central and convenient for travelling anywhere in singapore with a shopping centre and MRT below. Also right opposite is Raffles Hotel for your Singapore Sling in the Long Bar, but in my opinion the view from the New Asia Bar at the top of the Stamford is the best for a half price cocktail (including the infamous sling) from 3pm till 9pm, absolute bargain! Staff were efficient, friendly and helpfull , and the concerige not as stand offish as at some 5* hotels, we had a good laugh with them. The courtesy room was a great help, we had a key from 3pm when we checked out untill we left for the airport and didnt have to share at all. In additiion you can use the facilities at the Amirita Spa for free , lockers showers steram , sauna and spa pools for free if you are staying athe the Raffles Plaza,( its gorgeous!). We would definately use again, especially at the cheap rate we recieved from AsiaBesthote.com 拢81.00 a real bargain worth every penny as the breakfast was included and really set you up for the day.Food is so cheap in Singapore, about 拢3.00 a head will furnish a banquet at the cheap food courts found in most shopping centre hawker stalls, so unless you are a big alcohol drinker, dont bother with the executive rooms, deluxe is fine . Dont hesitate just book!

<Author>1stclasstravel
<Content>Get the South Tower Great hotel. Stayed here for 5 nights with no complaints. Great friendly service from the staff. Be sure to get a room in South Tower which includes a rain head shower. After a long hard day at work, a nice shower is one way to wind down. Has a spa, but I didn't try it out.Good workout facilities with plenty of treadmills, bikes and elliptical machines. A good variety of weight machines and a separate studio for stretching. If you get the breakfast package, the selection is pretty good. Comes with a juice bar. Great service. Always filling your coffee or tea cup. Location is very central to all the different malls that is connected to the hotel, so there is no need to go outside and be exposed to the heat and humidity. There is a food court in the Raffles City Center that offers decent food at really cheap prices. There is an underground link to the Esplanade. The Esplanade has some good restaurants with a water view. I tried No Signboard and had the chili crab. Yum! It's messy, but it's worth it. Be sure to call before going to see if you can get a table. I got there at 7:30 and got the last table right by the bus tray.Funan IT mall located on North Bridge Road is about a 5 minute walk from the hotel. Lots of electronic stores. Be sure to shop around, prices vary from place to place. I found Sim Lim to be cheaper.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Excellent city hotel We stayed at this hotel for 3 nights as part of our honeymoon. It exceeded my expectations in many areas. We followed the advice of many other tripadviser reviewers and booked a Raffles inc room in the South tower. The room was large, beautifully appointed with a view of the cricket ground and was very tastefully furnished. The bathroom was one of the best I have encountered in any hotel. A Bose wave radio and coffee machine were nice additions and the chocolates left on the pillow each night were delicious.The lounge was pleasant and although breakfast selection was more limited than eating at one of the restaurants, in this large hotel we appreciated the intimacy it provided. Only negative was some fellow guests overdoing it on cocktails during the free evening happy hour.The pool area was very average, being crowded and really quite noisy - bit of Club 18-30 feel and a contrast to the rest of our experience. I would, however, recommend a trip to the bar at the top of the adjacent sister hotel the Stamford - we arrived at the hotel at midnight, went straight there and it was an amazing start to a great stay in Singapore.

<Author>huxtable
<Content>adequate without being great My wife and I have just stayed here for 7 nightsI belief the following will help future travellers1. upgrade to a room in the South, new refurbished wing. These rooms are very good, bathrooms are magnificient with raindrop shower and white clean surfaces. Balconies with views either of Raffles, or the Harbour. The harbor views are superior, we were fortunate enough to stay in both room types.2. unless you are a business traveller or enjoy the pleasures of alcohol, you would be wasting your time and money getting a raffles inc room, for access to Raffles club3. breakfast is worth getting !There are three sites you can go for breakfastFor shere variety, the market cafe on level two of the south wing is the best4. Service throughout is below the standard I am used to in other Singapore hotels. This was the poorest off all 7 hotels I have stayed in Singapore. We got the clear impression from the service particularly at Raffles lounge ( see 2 ), that unless you were a business traveller of frequent customer, you were not worth as much care/concern5. the pool is pretty average for a 5 star establishment, and was always packed, I think this was because the pool is shared with the Stamford6. In terms of value for money, there are most certainly better hotels, eg fullerton, Intercontinental and the Ritz Carlton

<Author>AlexSanJose
<Content>Excellent  Based on other traveler's recommendations, stayed at the South Tower. Ended up staying a month and highly recommend the hotel. As others have mentioned, the South Tower furnishings are much newer. Ask for the higher floors for a better view. The rooms have floor to ceiling windows with a balcony that you can walk out on. The drapes are electrically controlled from the bedside. In fact all the lights in the room can be controlled from the bedside. Oh yes, the bedside control also handles the airconditioning. There is complementary a coffee maker. The closet has lights that turn on when the door is opened. The closet also has a safe and has robes and slippers to use. The bathroom has a dryer, a shower and a separate tub. Newspapers are delivered daily.The internet is extra and can be purchased by the day, the week or the month. I went for the weekly rate. The TV - not much selections, just one HBO station.My room came with the daily buffet breakfast. The buffet has a large selection, of western (omelet station, bacon, eggs, potatoes), pastries, Chinese, Japanese, fruits/cereal and wow a juice bar where you tell them what fruits to grind and voila - a juice combo of your choice.For cheap eats, the hotel is adjacent to a shopping mall where there is a very inexpensive food court on the second floor - cash and asian only. If you want western, then lower floor of the mall has various things like Subway, etc. Other restaurants in the mall, Hagen Daz ice cream, coffee bars, Indian food, Italian, Japanese, etc. The lower floor also has a supermarket if you want to get drinks or other stuff you want to bring to your room. And conveniently, the lower floor also has the debit/atm machines for getting cash.Around the hotel. Adjacent to the hotel is the Swissotel the Stamford that is connected via the mall. The Stamford is the tallest hotel in Singapore. And the real Raffles Hotel - The real colonial looking hotel is across the street from the lobby. The Chijmes bar area is also across the street. Lots of bars and different kinds of food. An Irish Pub for a pint of Guiness to middle eastern to Argentinian.Connected to the mall is the entrance to the MRT (train system) via an underground entrance. There is a whole world of shopping underground too. During the hot and humid weather above ground, the shoppin underground is cool. Walk the underground all the way to the Esplanade by the Bay about a twenty minute walk. An evening walk to see the harbor lights is recommended. If you go to the top of the Esplanade Theatre Building, you can take beatiful Night shots of the harbor.The river is only ten minutes if you walk above ground.The staff of the hotel is very helpful. They promptly provided an AC adaptor to convert my laptop plug for the room AC receptacle. The hotel also provided a large security cabinet to store my expensive equipment - no charge.Staying long term, laundry can be very pricey. The staff did not mind recommending a local laundry service that airline staff used. The service picked up and delivered to the hotel and charged half the hotel rate. And nicely enough, the hotel staff allowed the service to charge your account!The hotel is a very good value. Not as plush as Las Vegas or British Grand Hotels but something you cannot go wrong with.  
<Date>Oct 26, 2005

<Author>hazel
<Content>Great hotel My new husband and I stayed here on our way to Vietnam. We stayed for 5 nights and it was fantastic! On check in, we arrived at 6am, a bit frazzled after a 12 hour flight straight after the wedding and were given a room on the 17th floor. We had been told before arriving that we would have to pay for the night before to be able to check straight in but we weren't charged in the end. They provided us with a bowl of fruit on our first night. Each evening they would turn the bed down, leave delicious chocolates and turn the Bose stereo to play classical music when you arrived back - nice touch. The breakfast was exceptional, there was too much to list. I fell for the dim sum while hubby couldn't get enough of the American pancakes with ham and syrup. mmm. Good entertainment too - we watched a waiter drop a full tray of plates and the toaster caught fire another morning. You can also have bfast by the pool. The hotel is connected to the City Hall MRT which made getting to and from the airport a breeze for less than a pound each way. Singapore is a beautiful city, get out and do as much as you can, but I would recommend the luxury of the Plaza any day!!

<Content>Fantastic hotel... but get the renovated rooms I've stayed at Raffles The Plaza twice, once in the South Wing and once in the North Wing. From my experience, the room that I was in the South Wing far, far, far exceeded the quality of the room in the North Wing. So I was expecting the same this June after I convinced my sister and her boyfriend that it was the most amazing place. It was still of a fairly good quality, but you could tell that the carpeting was a bit tired, moisture had been taking a toll on the bathroom door, and they had shower curtains in the bath instead of a shower compartment. I hate those. Still, the high level of service was the same, nothing was too much trouble. Breakfast buffet was quite good. The best part of it is the location of the hotel... right at City Hall MRT. So all in all, I'd give this hotel a 5 star +++ rating for the fancy room in the South Wing and a 4 star for the room in the North Wing.

<Author>Barbarella
<Content>Wonderful hotel, great location We stayed at Raffles the Plaza 9-13 February this year and had a wonderful time. Our best decision was upgrading to an Executive Room which meant we could breakfast in the Executive Club which was a quiet and relaxing start to the day, and also enjoy the 'happy hour' from 5 - 8pm with free drinks and canapes, which we took full advantage of! Superb service in Executive Club with special thanks to Sara - you deserve an employee of the year award. Our room was madly luxurious, with the best hotel bathroom we have ever seen. There were a couple of small niggles though. The lighting system was controlled by a master switch by the bed but it seemed to have a mind of its own. We asked housekeeping to fix it, but it still didn't work so we gave up. And when we arrived, the TV remote plus one bathrobe were missing, and in spite of calling housekeeping twice it took them over an hour to supply the missing items. As my husband wanted to catch the evening news, he was not best pleased. The location of the hotel could not be bettered. It is built over a shopping centre and and MRT hub station so you can get anywhere you want in air-conditioned comfort (well, it can get a bit packed at weekends!). We bought an EZ Link card at the station which you can use on both metro and buses - very cheap and efficient, though taxis are a bargain as well.Glorious Raffles it just opposite the hotel - we had the obligatory Singapore Sling in the Long Bar and a wonderful romantic dinner in the courtyard. Singapore is a shoppers paradise but check prices at home if you are thinking of buying electronic goods - you may not get such a bargain as you think. We bartered long and hard over a video camera but found when we got home that we hadn't made such a huge saving and you can't return it if you have a problem.Do visit the Julong Bird Gardens (by MRT and bus) and the Botanic Gardens especially the sublime Orchid Garden. The Night Safari at the zoo is a must as well. You can book a trip like we did, but you don't have time to fit everything in so we would recommend public transport/taxi. And it took us over an hour to return to the hotel as we were the last to be dropped off - no fun at 11.30pm. There is so much to do and see (and spend your money on) in Singapore, four days was not nearly enough. We will be back - and we will definitely stay at Raffles the Plaza.  
<Date>Mar 30, 2005

<Author>EmmaNewZealand
<Content>great hotel once you upgrade We stayed here in March 2005 for 5 nights. We arribd late at night and the room we originally got was on the 6th floor of the North tower despite asking for a room in the south tower when our travel agent made the booking. The room was awful- it had not been refurbished and the whole floor smelt damp and musty. The bathroom had mould on the tile grouting between the bench and wall behind the sink. So the next day we asked to be put in the south tower- we had pay another $50 S a night but it was worth it. The room we got was on the 20th floor and overlooked the Raffles Hotel and the city beyond . The bathroom was modern and had a glass basin and benchtop- the monsoon shower was wonderful. We had delicious breakfasts every morning out by the lovely pool. We used the gym and the Amrita spa- all top class. Teh location was awesome and there is even a supermarket int he basement of the Raffles shopping centre- handy for buying water and snacks.We would definitely stay here again.

<Author>LHill
<Content>As good as it gets. This is a superb hotel, in every way. We stayed at the beginning of March, 2005, and found the Raffles Plaza to be the equal of any 4 or 5-star property we have stayed at anywhere in the world. Where are you going to find a Sony television and Bose radio in a hotel room? Breakfast in Cafe Mix provides a dizzying array of choices to suit every taste. The staff are excellent, location a brief 2 or 3 block walk through the historic district to the river or harbor, and only 4 or 5 blocks from the bargain markets of Chinatown. Previously in Singapore we have stayed at the Four Seasons, also a top hotel that we enjoyed, and, 25 years earlier stayed in the Ava Gardner suite of the original Raffles, when it still had its slightly shabby old colonial style. It is just across the street, and of course entirely renovated.For us, Singapore will now always be the Raffles Plaza.

<Author>RickyBon
<Content>Outstanding Hotel - Highly Recommended My fiancee and I stayed here for 3 nights in March 2005, and I can say that this is without doubt the best large hotel that we have ever stayed at.The levels of service from the moment that we arrived were unbelievable. Everyone was friendly, helpful and polite. I had booked a Premier Deluxe room in the South Tower and had requested a king size bed (which you are told on booking cannot be guaranteed). On arrival, the receptionist was highly apologetic and explained that she was unable to find a king size room for us, and so immediately upgraded us to an executive suite in the South Tower. We couldn't believe our luck, yet the receptionist kept thanking us for our understanding! The room on the 22nd floor was sensational - an amazing view out over the original Raffles hotel and for miles beyond, incredibly comfortable beds, widescreen TV, a brilliant touch of a Lavazza expresso machine and to cap it off, the best hotel bathroom I have ever seen with a glass sink and fantastic raindrop shower.The Amrita spa in the hotel was free to guests and the facilities wonderful. Massages and other treatments were excellent and all very affordable. The hotel pool was also excellent.I cannot emphasise how good the location of this hotel is. It is attached to the huge Raffles City shopping complex close to its MRT underground station for exploring the rest of the City (Chinatown, Little India and Orchard Road only 2 or 3 stops away), and is next door to the great bars and restaurants of CHIJMES, with the Raffles Long Bar across the road for the essential Singapore Sling. On checking out at 1.30pm, we mentioned to the receptionist that we were not flying out of Changi until the early hours - we were immediately offered ongoing free use of the spa facilities until 11pm and our own hospitality lounge. A lovely touch when most hotels just want to get rid of you!This is the first hotel at I have stayed at where it feels as though every small detail has been thought of - I will be staying again and would highly recommend it to all other users.  
<Date>Mar 6, 2005
